    <td>\n         <span class="url">\n          <a class="external text" href="http://www.cityofmyrtlebeach.com" rel="nofollow">\n           www\n           <wbr/>\n           .cityofmyrtlebeach\n           <wbr/>\n           .com\n          </a>\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Myrtle Beach\n       </b>\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">\n         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">\n          /\n          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">\n           <span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\n            \xcb\x88\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'m\' in \'my\'">\n            m\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x9c\xcb\x90r/: \'ur\' in \'fur\'">\n            \xc9\x9c\xcb\x90r\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'t\' in \'tie\'">\n            t\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x99/: \'a\' in \'about\'">\n            \xc9\x99\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'l\' in \'lie\'">\n            l\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\n            \xcb\x88\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'b\' in \'buy\'">\n            b\n           </span>\n           <span title="/i\xcb\x90/: \'ee\' in \'fleece\'">\n            i\xcb\x90\n           </span>\n           <span title="/t\xca\x83/: \'ch\' in \'China\'">\n            t\xca\x83\n           </span>\n          </span>\n          /\n         </a>\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       is a coastal city on the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        east coast\n       </a>\n       of the United States in\n       <a href="/wiki/Horry_County,_South_Carolina" title="Horry County, South Carolina">\n        Horry County\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </a>\n       . It is situated on the center of a large and continuous stretch of beach known as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Strand" title="Grand Strand">\n        Grand Strand\n       </a>\n       in northeastern South Carolina.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach is one of the major centers of tourism in South Carolina and the United States because of the city\'s warm subtropical climate and extensive beaches, attracting an estimated 14 million visitors each year.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of the 2010 census, the population of the city was 27,109 with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_metropolitan_area" title="Myrtle Beach metropolitan area">\n        Myrtle Beach metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       population at 465,391 according to a 2013 estimate.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#History">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           1\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           History\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2">\n         <a href="#Geography">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           2\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Geography\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-9">\n         <a href="#Economy">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Economy\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-10">\n           <a  <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-11">\n             <a href="#Thong_bikini_ban">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               4.1.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Thong bikini ban\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-12">\n             <a href="#Motorcycle_rallies">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               4.1.2\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Motorcycle rallies\n class="tocnumber">\n             4.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Shopping\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-14">\n         <a href="#Sports">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Sports\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15">\n           <a href="#Golf">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             5.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Golf\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-16">\n         <a href="#Government">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           6\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Government\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-17">\n           <a href="#Mayors">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n       <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-21">\n             <a href="#Private_Schools_and_Charter_Schools">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               7.1.2\n              </span>\n class="toclevel-2 tocsection-22">\n           <a href="#Higher_education">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             7.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n class="tocnumber">\n           8\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Media\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 class="tocnumber">\n             9.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Transportation\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-29">\n             <a href="#Air">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n               9.1.1\n              </span>\n              <span class="toctext">\n               Air\n              </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-30">\n             <a href="#Rail">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n        </span>\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-32">\n             <a href="#Mass_transit">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n   <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-33">\n           <a href="#Healthcare">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             9.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="History">\n        History\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FGBurroughs.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="377" data-file-width="591" height="140" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/FGBurroughs.jpg/220px-FGBurroughs.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/FGBurroughs.jpg/330px-FGBurroughs.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/FGBurroughs.jpg/440px-FGBurroughs.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FGBurroughs.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Burroughs_%26_Chapin" title="Burroughs &amp; Chapin">\n          F.G. Burroughs\n         </a>\n         steamship\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="522" data-file-width="750" height="153" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg/220px-Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg/330px-Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg/440px-Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mbaaf-1943-1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Original Myrtle Beach Air Force Base during\n         <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">\n          World War II\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1378" data-file-width="2584" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG/220px-Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG/330px-Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG/440px-Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Rainbow_Court_Myrtle_Beach_SC_Jun_10.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Rainbow_Court" title="Rainbow Court">\n          Rainbow Court\n         </a>\n         (1935 to 1959) is listed on the\n         <a href="/wiki/National_Register_of_Historic_Places_listings_in_Horry_County,_South_Carolina" title="National Register of Historic Places listings in Horry County, South Carolina">\n          National Register of Historic Places\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Fighting_Stallions.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="314" data-file-width="405" height="171" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Fighting_Stallions.JPG/220px-Fighting_Stallions.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Fighting_Stallions.JPG/330px-Fighting_Stallions.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/92/Fighting_Stallions.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Fighting_Stallions.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Brookgreen_Gardens" title="Brookgreen Gardens">\n          Brookgreen Gardens\n         </a>\n         sculpture park (1932) in\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Murrells_Inlet" title="Murrells Inlet">\n          Murrells Inlet\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Prior to the arrival of Europeans, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Strand" title="Grand Strand">\n        Long Bay\n       </a>\n       area was inhabited by the native\n       <a href="/wiki/Waccamaw" title="Waccamaw">\n        Waccamaw\n       </a>\n       Tribe. The Waccamaw used the river for travel and fished along the shore around\n       <a href="/wiki/Little_River,_South_Carolina" title="Little River, South Carolina">\n        Little River\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/Waties_Island,_South_Carolina" title="Waties Island, South Carolina">\n        Waties Island\n       </a>\n       , the primary barrier island along Long Bay, has evidence of burial and shell mounds, remains of the visiting Waccamaw.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The first European settler along Long Bay arrived in the late 18th Century, attempting to extend the\n       <a href="/wiki/Plantation_economy" title="Plantation economy">\n        plantation system\n       </a>\n       outward towards the ocean.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Records are sparse from this period, with most of the recorded history pieced together from old\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Land_grants" title="Land grants">\n        land grants\n       </a>\n       documents.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       These settlers were met with mixed results, producing unremarkable quantities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Indigo" title="Indigo">\n        indigo\n       </a>\n       and tobacco as the coast\'s soil was sandy and most of the crop yields were of an inferior quality.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Prior to the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Revolution" title="American Revolution">\n        American Revolution\n       </a>\n       , the area along the future Grand Strand was essentially uninhabited. Several families received land grants along the coast, including the Witherses: John, Richard, William, and Mary. This family received an area around present-day Wither\'s Swash, also known as Myrtle Swash or the eight-Mile Swash. A separate grant was granted to James Minor, including a barrier island named Minor Island, now\n       <a href="/wiki/Waties_Island,_South_Carolina" title="Waties Island, South Carolina">\n        Waties Island\n       </a>\n       , off of the coast near Little River.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Mary Wither\'s gravestone at\n       <a href="/wiki/Prince_George_Winyah_Episcopal_Church" title="Prince George Winyah Episcopal Church">\n        Prince George Winyah Episcopal Church\n       </a>\n       speaks to the remoteness of the former Strand: "She gave up the pleasures of Society and retired to Long Bay, where she resided a great part of her life devoted to the welfare of her children."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As the American colonies gained independence, the area remained essentially unchanged, and the coast remained barren.\n       <a href="/wiki/George_Washington" title="George Washington">\n        George Washington\n       </a>\n       scouted out the Southern states during his term, traveling down the\n       <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Highway_(Charleston_to_Boston)" title="King\'s Highway (Charleston to Boston)">\n        King\'s Highway\n       </a>\n       . He stayed a night at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Windy_Hill_Beach" title="Windy Hill Beach">\n        Windy Hill\n       </a>\n       (part of present-day\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Myrtle_Beach" title="North Myrtle Beach">\n        North Myrtle Beach\n       </a>\n       ) and was led across Wither\'s Swash to\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgetown,_South_Carolina" title="Georgetown, South Carolina">\n        Georgetown\n       </a>\n       by Jeremiah Vereen.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Withers family remained one of the few settlers around Myrtle Beach for the next half-century. In 1822, a strong hurricane swept the house of R. F. Withers into the ocean, drowning 18 people inside. The tragedy made the Withers family decide to abandon their plots along the coast.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Left unattended, the area began to return to forest.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Burroughs and Collins Company of Conway, predecessor of modern-day\n       <a href="/wiki/Burroughs_%26_Chapin" title="Burroughs &amp; Chapin">\n        Burroughs &amp; Chapin\n       </a>\n       , purchased much of the Withers\xe2\x80\x99 family land in 1881, and the growing community was called New Town around the start of the 20th century. A\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">\n        post office\n       </a>\n       named "Withers" to serve the site of the old Swash in 1888. On February 28, 1899 Burroughs and Collins received a charter to build the Conway &amp; Seashore Railroad to transport timber from the coast to inland customers. The railroad began daily service on May 1, 1900 with two wood-burning locomotives. One of the engines was dubbed\n       <i>\n        The Black Maria\n       </i>\n       and came second-hand from a North Carolina logging operation.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After the railroad was finished, employees of the lumber and railroad company would take train\n       <a href="/wiki/Flatcar" title="Flatcar">\n        flatcars\n       </a>\n       down to beach area on their free weekends, becoming the first Grand Strand tourists.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The railroad terminus was nicknamed "New Town", contrasting it with the "Old Town", or\n       <a href="/wiki/Conway,_South_Carolina" title="Conway, South Carolina">\n        Conway\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Around the start of the 20th century,\n       <a href="/wiki/Franklin_Burroughs_(businessman)" title="Franklin Burroughs (businessman)">\n        Franklin Burroughs\n       </a>\n       envisioned turning New Town into a tourist destination rivaling the Florida and northeastern beaches. Burroughs died in 1897, but his sons completed the railroad\'s expansion to the beach and opened the Seaside Inn in 1901.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Around 1900, a contest was held to name the area and Burroughs\' wife suggested honoring the locally abundant shrub, the Southern Wax Myrtle (\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Myrica_cerifera" title="Myrica cerifera">\n         Myrica cerifera\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       ). The Withers post office changed its name to Myrtle Beach soon afterward. It incorporated as a town in 1938 and as a city in 1957.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 1937, Myrtle Beach Municipal Airport was built, however it was promptly taken over by the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Corps" title="United States Army Air Corps">\n        United States Army Air Corps\n       </a>\n       in 1940 and converted into a\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Air_Force_Base" title="Myrtle Beach Air Force Base">\n        military base\n       </a>\n       . Commercial flights began in 1976 and shared the runway for over 15 years until the air base closed in 1993. Since then the airport has been named\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_International_Airport" title="Myrtle Beach International Airport">\n        Myrtle Beach International Airport\n       </a>\n       . In 2010 plans to build a new terminal were approved. In 1940, Kings Highway was finally paved, giving Myrtle Beach its first primary highway.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Myrtle_Heights-Oak_Park_Historic_District" title="Myrtle Heights-Oak Park Historic District">\n        Myrtle Heights-Oak Park Historic District\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Atlantic_Coast_Line_Railroad_Station" title="Myrtle Beach Atlantic Coast Line Railroad Station">\n        Myrtle Beach Atlantic Coast Line Railroad Station\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_Forest_Country_Club" title="Ocean Forest Country Club">\n        Ocean Forest Country Club\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pleasant_Inn" title="Pleasant Inn">\n        Pleasant Inn\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainbow_Court" title="Rainbow Court">\n        Rainbow Court\n       </a>\n       are listed on the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Register_of_Historic_Places" title="National Register of Historic Places">\n        National Register of Historic Places\n       </a>\n       . Also listed was the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesterfield_Inn" title="Chesterfield Inn">\n        Chesterfield Inn\n       </a>\n       , now demolished.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nris_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nris-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The demolished\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Pavilion" title="Myrtle Beach Pavilion">\n        Myrtle Beach Pavilion\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/Gay_Dolphin_Gift_Cove" title="Gay Dolphin Gift Cove">\n        Gay Dolphin Gift Cove\n       </a>\n       on the Boardwalk was built in 1946, and sells seashells and Myrtle Beach souvenirs. It claims to be the "nation\'s largest gift shop."\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">\n        Geography\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       A\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Man-made_island" title="Man-made island">\n        man-made island\n       </a>\n       , Myrtle Beach has been separated from the continental United States since 1936 by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Intracoastal_Waterway" title="Intracoastal Waterway">\n        Intracoastal Waterway\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       forcing the city and area in general to develop within a small distance from the coast. In part due to this separation, the area directly west of Myrtle Beach across the waterway remained primarily rural, whereas its northern and southern ends were bordered by other developed tourist towns,\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina" title="North Myrtle Beach, South Carolina">\n        North Myrtle Beach\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Surfside_Beach,_South_Carolina" title="Surfside Beach, South Carolina">\n        Surfside Beach\n       </a>\n       . Since then, the inland portion of the Myrtle Beach area has developed dramatically and the beach itself is developing westward.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       According to the United States Census Bureau, the city has a total area of 23.55 square miles (61.0\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Neighborhoods">\n        Neighborhoods\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Neighborhoods">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 12em; -webkit-column-width: 12em; column-width: 12em;">\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         Arcadian Shores\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         Benton Park\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         Booker T.    <li>\n         Washington Park\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         Withers Preserve\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         Withers Swash\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         Yaupon Circle\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">\n        Climate\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Climate">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       According to the\n       <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification">\n        K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification\n       </a>\n       , Myrtle Beach has a\n       <a href="/wiki/Humid_subtropical_climate" title="Humid subtropical climate">\n        humid subtropical climate\n       </a>\n       or Cfa \xe2\x80\x93 typical of the Gulf and South Atlantic states. The city enjoys abundant sunshine year-round with more than 2800 hours annually.\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sand_Dunes.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Sand_Dunes.jpg/220px-Sand_Dunes.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Sand_Dunes.jpg/330px-Sand_Dunes.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Sand_Dunes.jpg/440px-Sand_Dunes.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sand_Dunes.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Myrtle Beach is protected from erosion by vegetation-filled\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sand_dunes" title="Sand dunes">\n          sand dunes\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The summer season is long, hot, and humid in Myrtle Beach. Average daytime highs are from 83 to 91\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (28 to 33\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and average night-time lows are near 70\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (21\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). The coastal location of Myrtle Beach mitigates summer heat\n       <i>\n        somewhat\n       </i>\n       compared to inland areas of South Carolina: Thus, while nearby\n       <a href="/wiki/Florence,_South_Carolina" title="Florence, South Carolina">\n        Florence\n       </a>\n       averages 65 days annually with high temperatures of 90\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F or higher \xe2\x80\x93 Myrtle Beach averages only 21. The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bermuda_High" title="Bermuda High">\n        Bermuda High\n       </a>\n       pumps in humidity from the tropical Atlantic toward Myrtle Beach, giving summers a near tropical feel in the city. The warm Atlantic Ocean reaches 80\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F or higher in the summer months off Myrtle Beach, making for warm and sultry summer nights. Summer thunderstorms are common in the hot season in Myrtle Beach, and the summer months from June through September have the most\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Precipitation_(meteorology)" title="Precipitation (meteorology)">\n        precipitation\n       </a>\n       . In summer, thunderstorms normally build during the heat of the day \xe2\x80\x93 followed by brief and intense downpours.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach has mostly mild winters of short duration: Average daytime highs range from 57 to 61\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (14 \xe2\x80\x93 16\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and nighttime lows are in the 36 to 38\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (2 \xe2\x80\x93 3\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) from December through February. Winter temperatures vary more than summer temperatures in Myrtle Beach: Some winters can see several cold days with highs only in the upper 40s F (7 \xe2\x80\x93 9\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), while other winter days can see highs in the upper 60s and low 70s F (19 \xe2\x80\x93 23\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). Myrtle Beach averages 33 days annually with\n       <a href="/wiki/Frost" title="Frost">\n        frost\n       </a>\n       , though in some years less than 15 days will see frost. Snowfall is very rare in Myrtle Beach, however a few times every 15 or 20 years a trace of snow might fall. In February 2010, a rare 2.8 inches (71\xc2\xa0mm) of snow fell in Myrtle Beach. The spring (March, April and May) and fall (September, October and November) months are normally mild and sunny in Myrtle Beach, with high temperatures in the 60s and 70s. The beach season in Myrtle Beach normally runs from late April through late October. SST (\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_Surface_Temperature" title="Sea Surface Temperature">\n        Sea Surface Temperatures\n       </a>\n       ) are often in the lower 80\'s (26 \xe2\x80\x93 28\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) off South Carolina in summer and early fall.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Summer thunderstorms can be severe, but are brief, but tornadoes are rare in Myrtle Beach.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclones" title="Tropical cyclones">\n        Tropical cyclones\n       </a>\n       occasionally impact Myrtle Beach, though weaker tropical storms and weak tropical lows are more common. Like most areas prone to tropical cyclones, a direct hit by a major hurricane is infrequent in Myrtle Beach. The last hurricane to cause significant damage in Myrtle Beach was\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hugo" title="Hurricane Hugo">\n        Hurricane Hugo\n       </a>\n       in 1989. The worst hurricane in the history of Myrtle Beach was\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hazel" title="Hurricane Hazel">\n        Hurricane Hazel\n       </a>\n       in 1954.\n      </p>\n      <div style="width: 100%;">\n       <table class="wikitable collapsible" style="width:90%; text-align:center; font-size:90%; line-height: 1.2em; margin:auto;">\n        <tr>\n         <th colspan="14">\n   Myrtle Beach is the largest principal city of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach-Conway-Georgetown,_SC_CSA" title="Myrtle Beach-Conway-Georgetown, SC CSA">\n        Myrtle Beach-Conway-Georgetown CSA\n       </a>\n       , a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Combined_Statistical_Area" title="Combined Statistical Area">\n        Combined Statistical Area\n       </a>\n       that includes the\n       <a href="/wiki/Horry_County,_South_Carolina" title="Horry County, South Carolina">\n        Myrtle Beach-Conway-North Myrtle Beach metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       (Horry County) and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgetown_County,_South_Carolina" title="Georgetown County, South Carolina">\n        Georgetown micropolitan area\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgetown_County,_South_Carolina" title="Georgetown County, South Carolina">\n        Georgetown County\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which had a combined population of 329,449 at the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Census,_2010" title="United States Census, 2010">\n        2010 census\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GR8_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GR8-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of the 2010 census, the population of Myrtle Beach was 27,109.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GR8_19-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GR8-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Per the 2000 census\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GR2_1-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GR2-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       there were 22,759 permanent residents in Myrtle Beach, 10,413 households, 5,414 families, 1,356.5 people per square mile (523.7/km\xc2\xb2), with 14,658 housing units at an average density of 873.5 per square mile (337.3/km\xc2\xb2).\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ethnicities">\n        Ethnicities\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a      ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The racial makeup of the city was:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        72.3% white\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        13.9%\n        <a href="/wiki/Race_and_ethnicity_in_the_United_States_Census" title="Race and ethnicity in the United States Census">\n         Black\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        0.7%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Native_American_(U.S._Census)" title="Native American (U.S. Census)">\n         Native American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        1.5%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_(U.S._Census)" title="Asian (U.S. Census)">\n         Asian\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        0.3%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Islander_(U.S._Census)" title="Pacific Islander (U.S. Census)">\n         Pacific Islander\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        8.7% from\n races.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hispanic_(U.S._Census)" title="Hispanic (U.S. Census)">\n         Hispanic\n        </a>\n        or\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latino_(U.S._Census)" title="Latino (U.S. Census)">\n         Latino\n        </a>\n        of any race were 13.7% of the population.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Age">\n        Age\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Of the total Myrtle Beach population:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        18.0% were 1\xe2\x80\x9317\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        11.0% were between 18\xe2\x80\x9324\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        33.6% were between 25\xe2\x80\x9344\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        22.5% were between 45\xe2\x80\x9364\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        15.0% were 65 or older\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Median age was 37 years\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        103 males per 100 females overall\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        101 males per 100 females age 18 and over\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Income">\n        Income\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Income">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Overall median income for a household in the city was $35,498\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Median income for a family was $43,900\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Males had a median income of $26,039\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Females had a median income of $22,473\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The per capita income for the city was $23,214.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        About 7.6% of families and 12.0% of the population were below the poverty line, including 17.1% of those under age 18 and 6.6% of those age 65 or over.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">\n        Economy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Economy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="530" data-file-width="480" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png/170px-Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png/255px-Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png/340px-Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Margate_Tower_6-7-17.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The 29-floor Margate Hotel Tower is the tallest building in Myrtle Beach\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach\'s economy is dominated by the tourist industry;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       hotels, motels, resorts, restaurants, attractions, and retail developments exist in abundance to service visitors.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There are approximately 95 golf courses in and around Myrtle Beach (as of 2015) as the golfing industry represents a significant presence in the area.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A manufacturing base produces plastic, rubber, cardboard, foam, and ceramic products usually in small scale.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">\n        Tourism\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Tourism">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1728" data-file-width="2592" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg/220px-Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg/330px-Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg/440px-Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Myrtle-Beach-SC-0799.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Myrtle Beach (July 2014)\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Hosting over 14 million visitors annually, the Grand Strand is home to an array of tourist attractions, and the area receives a large influx of visitors during all seasons. Nearly 100,000 visitors a year are estimated to come from overseas, with tourists from Canada, Germany and the United Kingdom.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Myrtle_Beach_Hotels_and_Tourism_21-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Myrtle_Beach_Hotels_and_Tourism-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_attractions_in_Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina" title="List of attractions in Myrtle Beach, South Carolina">\n        List of attractions in Myrtle Beach, South Carolina\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach hosts a variety of special conventions, events, and musical concerts. The area\'s attractions include its beaches and courses, as well as a number of amusement parks, an aquarium,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legends_In_Concert" title="Legends In Concert">\n        Legends In Concert\n       </a>\n       , retail developments, a number of shopping complexes and over 1,900 restaurants\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-myrtlebeachareachamber.com_22-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-myrtlebeachareachamber.com-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       including seafood restaurants. The area also has dinner theaters, nightclubs, and many tourist shops. Myrtle Beach has an estimated 460 hotels, with many on the beachfront, and approximately 89,000 accommodation units in total. Also in the city is\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Waves" title="Myrtle Waves">\n        Myrtle Waves\n       </a>\n       , one of the largest water parks on the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        East Coast of the United States\n       </a>\n       . Myrtle Beach has the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sun_Fun_Festival" title="Sun Fun Festival">\n        Sun Fun Festival\n       </a>\n       early each June.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Carolina_Opry" title="The Carolina Opry">\n        The Carolina Opry\n       </a>\n       is another highly acclaimed attraction, which features various musical, comedy, dance, and entertainment shows, including the Carolina Opry (variety show), Good Vibrations (best of the 1960s, 1970s, and 1980s), Light\xe2\x80\x94a Laser Extravaganza. During the holiday season, the venue hosts the Carolina Opry Christmas Special. It is housed in a 2,200-seat theater.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Boardwalk" title="Myrtle Beach Boardwalk">\n        Myrtle Beach Boardwalk\n       </a>\n       opened in 2010 and has been recognized as the nation\'s #3 boardwalk by\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/National_Geographic_Society" title="National Geographic Society">\n         National Geographic\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and one of the best US boardwalks by\n       <a href="/wiki/Travel_%2B_Leisure" title="Travel + Leisure">\n        Travel + Leisure magazine\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Myrtle Beach Skywheel opened at the boardwalk in May, 2011, and is a 200-foot (61\xc2\xa0m) observation wheel, similar to a ferris wheel, with glass gondolas that look over the Atlantic Ocean. This is the first wheel of its kind in the U.S.\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_State_Park" title="Myrtle Beach State Park">\n        Myrtle Beach State Park\n       </a>\n       , established in 1935, has just under a mile of Grand Strand beach and is a prime location for camping, swimming, hiking, biking, and fishing.\n       <a href="/wiki/Pier_14" title="Pier 14">\n        Pier 14\n       </a>\n       by the Boardwalk.\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image"  </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Boardwalk" title="Myrtle Beach Boardwalk">\n          Myrtle Beach Boardwalk\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div      <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Splashes_Oceanfront_Water_Park.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Family_Kingdom_Amusement_Park_3.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage"        <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Family_Kingdom_Amusement_Park_3.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Family_Kingdom_Amusement_Park" title="Family Kingdom Amusement Park">\n          Family Kingdom Amusement Park\n         </a>\n         opened in 1966\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Convention_Center" title="Myrtle Beach Convention Center">\n        Myrtle Beach Convention Center\n       </a>\n       is a large facility that hosts a variety of meetings, conferences, exhibits, and special events every year. The expansive center, which opened in 2003, has a\n       <a href="/wiki/Sheraton_Hotels_and_Resorts" title="Sheraton Hotels and Resorts">\n        Sheraton\n       </a>\n       hotel and resort.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach welcomed\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hard_Rock_Park" title="Hard Rock Park">\n        Hard Rock Park\n       </a>\n       in 2008, which was themed after the popular\n       <a href="/wiki/Hard_Rock_Cafe" title="Hard Rock Cafe">\n        Hard Rock Cafe\n       </a>\n       chain. After financial issues, the park became Freestyle Music Park for the 2009 season. The park features attractions themed after various genres and eras of music, such as the\n       <a href="/wiki/British_Invasion" title="British Invasion">\n        British Invasion\n       </a>\n       . The park did not open for the 2010 season, and continues to be closed due to having been engulfed in legal issues. As of 2014, the park has been closed and is being dismantled.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Each March since 1951 during Ontario\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Spring_break" title="Spring break">\n        spring break\n       </a>\n       , Myrtle Beach has hosted Canadian-American Days, also known as Can-Am Days. Tens of thousands of tourists flock to the area for a week\'s worth of special events.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Myrtle Beach is also home to Coastal Uncorked, a food and wine festival held in the late spring annually. In June, recently graduated high school seniors come to Myrtle Beach for\n       <a href="/wiki/Senior_Week" title="Senior Week">\n        Senior Week\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       With numerous professional fireworks displays along the oceanfront, Myrtle Beach is recognized among the top destinations for Fourth of July travel.\n       <a href="/wiki/Priceline.com" title="Priceline.com">\n        Priceline.com\n       </a>\n       ranked Myrtle Beach among its top 20 destinations for Fourth of July in 2010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The majority of visitors make their way to the region during the high season (June\xe2\x80\x93August) looking to make the most of its fine weather.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Although gambling is not legal in South Carolina, Myrtle Beach residents and visitors have easy access to gambling by boat, as passengers can travel into international waters beyond the reach of federal and state gambling laws.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The city and surrounding area is served by Myrtle Beach International Airport. With regular flights to and from destinations such as Atlanta, Boston, Detroit, Fort Lauderdale, New York and Washington, the airport itself is well connected for both domestic and international tourists visiting the region. The airport also serves as a seasonal gateway to and from the likes of Chicago, Dallas and Toronto.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The city is located between\n       <a href="/wiki/Wilmington,_North_Carolina" title="Wilmington, North Carolina">\n        Wilmington, North Carolina\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Charleston,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston, South Carolina">\n        Charleston, South Carolina\n       </a>\n       with\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_17" title="U.S. Route 17">\n        U.S. Route 17\n       </a>\n       serving as the main transport link for those journeying from the north and south.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Myrtle_Beach_Hotels_and_Tourism_21-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Myrtle_Beach_Hotels_and_Tourism-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Thong_bikini_ban">\n        Thong bikini ban\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Thong bikini ban">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Thong_(clothing)" title="Thong (clothing)">\n        Thongs\n       </a>\n       (or any swimwear revealing any portion of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Buttocks" title="Buttocks">\n        buttocks\n       </a>\n       ) are not permitted anywhere in public in Myrtle Beach, including all beaches.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-myrtle_beach_thong_ban_28-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-myrtle_beach_thong_ban-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Violators of the ban may be arrested, jailed, or fined.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city\'s "thong ordinance" has been in effect since the 1990s.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Motorcycle_rallies">\n        Motorcycle rallies\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Motorcycle rallies">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="333" data-file-width="500" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg/220px-Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg/330px-Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg/440px-Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Yellow_and_black_and_silver_Suzukis_Black_Bike_Week_2008.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Riders in traffic at the 2008\n         <a href="/wiki/Black_Bike_Week" title="Black Bike Week">\n          Atlantic Beach Bikefest\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach Bike Week, also called "Harley Bike Week" is a week-long\n       <a href="/wiki/Motorcycle_rally" title="Motorcycle rally">\n        motorcycle rally\n       </a>\n       first held in 1940, the same year Kings Highway was paved.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The event has attracted as many as 200,000 visitors to the city every May.\n       <a href="/wiki/Black_Bike_Week" title="Black Bike Week">\n        Black Bike Week\n       </a>\n       , founded in 1980, takes place the weekend around Memorial Day Weekend and is the largest African American motorcycle rally in the US and attracts as many as 400,000 visitors. The event was created in response to a history of discrimination against African-American visitors and riders to Myrtle Beach and the Grand Strand Area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rallies1_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rallies1-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Myrtle Beach government created 15 new laws aimed at preventing all sanctioned motorcycle events within the city in response to controversy including accusations of racism by African-American riders during their event and complaints of lawlessness and poor behavior during all highly attended events. Several lawsuits by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Association_for_the_Advancement_of_Colored_People" title="National Association for the Advancement of Colored People">\n        National Association for the Advancement of Colored People\n       </a>\n       (NAACP) against Myrtle Beach businesses were settled with agreements that discrimination cease, compensation be given to some plaintiffs, and employees be given diversity training.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GroupLawsuits_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GroupLawsuits-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The NAACP suit against the City of Myrtle Beach was settled in 2006 without the city paying damages, but with the agreement police would use the same traffic control rules during both the black and the white motorcycle rallies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MBrelease_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MBrelease-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina_Supreme_Court" title="South Carolina Supreme Court">\n        South Carolina Supreme Court\n       </a>\n       in June 2010 unanimously overturned one of the 15 ordinances, which had required all motorcyclists to wear\n       <a href="/wiki/Motorcycle_helmet" title="Motorcycle helmet">\n        helmets\n       </a>\n       , on the grounds that the state law, requiring helmets only for riders under age 21, cannot be preempted by a city ordinance. In addition, the Court ruled, the ordinance created undue confusion, and that the city itself had invalidated their own helmet law and some other ordinances in a subsequent amendment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harley2010_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Harley2010-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The law had been challenged by a group of motorcyclists and a group of Myrtle Beach businesses called BOOST, Business Owners Organized to Support Tourism, who opposed the city\'s anti-motorcycle tourism policy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TourismPolicy_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TourismPolicy-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shopping">\n        Shopping\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Shopping">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2972" data-file-width="3759" height="174" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg/220px-Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg/330px-Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg/440px-Myrtle_Beach%2C_South_Carolina.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Myrtle Beach is home to a large number of beachwear shops\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Alabamatheatre.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="4000" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Alabamatheatre.JPG/220px-Alabamatheatre.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Alabamatheatre.JPG/330px-Alabamatheatre.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Alabamatheatre.JPG/440px-Alabamatheatre.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Alabamatheatre.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Alabama_Theatre_(Myrtle_Beach)" title="Alabama Theatre (Myrtle Beach)">\n          Alabama Theatre\n         </a>\n         at Barefoot Landing\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach has many stores and malls, is one of the largest shopping areas in the Southeastern United States\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       , and is the largest shopping destination in South Carolina\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Coastal_Grand_Mall" title="Coastal Grand Mall">\n         Coastal Grand Mall\n        </a>\n        opened in 2004 and is one of the largest indoor malls in the state\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n        . The mall, which has indoor and outdoor shopping areas, has a gross leasable area of 1,047,732 square feet (97,337.5\xc2\xa0m\n        <sup>\n         2\n        </sup>\n        ). The single-story facility has five anchor stores (including\n        <a href="/wiki/Sears" title="Sears">\n         Sears\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Belk" title="Belk">\n         Belk\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JCPenney" title="JCPenney">\n         JCPenney\n        </a>\n        , and\n        <a href="/wiki/Dillard%27s" title="Dillard\'s">\n         Dillard\'s\n        </a>\n        ), a 14-screen movie theater, a food court, and roughly 170 stores in total.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Mall" title="Myrtle Beach Mall">\n         Myrtle Beach Mall\n        </a>\n        is 525,385 square feet (48,809.9\xc2\xa0m\n        <sup>\n         2\n        </sup>\n        ), and has three anchor stores,\n        <a href="/wiki/Bass_Pro_Shops" title="Bass Pro Shops">\n         Bass Pro Shops\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Belk" title="Belk">\n         Belk\n        </a>\n        and\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JCPenney" title="JCPenney">\n         JCPenney\n        </a>\n        . The single-story mall also has a 12-screen movie theater, a food court, and other specialty stores. It used to be known as Colonial Mall, and was built as Briarcliffe Mall.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tanger_Outlets" title="Tanger Outlets">\n         Tanger Outlets\n        </a>\n        is a shopping outlet center. There are two locations, one near\n        <a href="/wiki/Briarcliffe_Acres,_South_Carolina" title="Briarcliffe Acres, South Carolina">\n         Briarcliffe Acres\n        </a>\n        and one near\n        <a href="/wiki/Carolina_Forest,_South_Carolina" title="Carolina Forest, South Carolina">\n         Carolina Forest\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n         <a href="#cite_note-40">\n          [40]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Broadway_at_the_Beach" title="Broadway at the Beach">\n         Broadway at the Beach\n        </a>\n        is a shopping complex set on 350 acres (1.4\xc2\xa0km\n        <sup>\n         2\n        </sup>\n        ) along the\n        <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_17_in_South_Carolina" title="U.S. Route 17 in South Carolina">\n         U.S. 17 Bypass\n        </a>\n        surrounding the 23-acre (93,000\xc2\xa0m\n        <sup>\n         2\n        </sup>\n        ) Lake Broadway. It is the largest festival entertainment complex in South Carolina.\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2016)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Barefoot_Landing" title="Barefoot Landing">\n         Barefoot Landing\n        </a>\n        is an outdoor shopping complex that consists of several divided sections located on filled land over top of Louis Lake, next to the Intracoastal Waterway. It contains many stores and attractions such as\n        <a href="/wiki/House_of_Blues" title="House of Blues">\n         House of Blues\n        </a>\n        (opened in 1997) and the\n        <a href="/wiki/Alabama_Theatre_(Myrtle_Beach)" title="Alabama Theatre (Myrtle Beach)">\n         Alabama Theatre\n        </a>\n        . Opened in 1988.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Market_Common" title="The Market Common">\n         The Market Common\n        </a>\n        is a\n        <a href="/wiki/Lifestyle_center_(retail)" title="Lifestyle center (retail)">\n         lifestyle district\n        </a>\n        housing several upscale retail and apartments. It is located on the site of the former\n        <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Air_Force_Base" title="Myrtle Beach Air Force Base">\n         Myrtle Beach Air Force Base\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Sports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg/220px-NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg/330px-NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg/440px-NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NASCAR_Racing_Experience_24.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Speedway" title="Myrtle Beach Speedway">\n          Myrtle Beach Speedway\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Myrtlewood.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Myrtlewood.JPG/220px-Myrtlewood.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Myrtlewood.JPG/330px-Myrtlewood.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Myrtlewood.JPG/440px-Myrtlewood.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Myrtlewood.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The Myrtlewood Golf Club\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Myrtle Beach is home to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Pelicans" title="Myrtle Beach Pelicans">\n        Myrtle Beach Pelicans\n       </a>\n       , a\n       <a href="/wiki/Carolina_League" title="Carolina League">\n        Carolina League\n       </a>\n       baseball team, a\n       <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Cubs" title="Chicago Cubs">\n        Chicago Cubs\n       </a>\n       farm franchise and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_FC" title="Myrtle Beach FC">\n        Myrtle Beach FC\n       </a>\n       , a pro soccer team playing in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Premier_Development_League" title="Premier Development League">\n        Premier Development League\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       From 1998-2009 and again starting in 2011 (no Saturday races were held in 2010 due to snow), the area hosted the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/BI-LO_(United_States)" title="BI-LO (United States)">\n         Bi-Lo\n        </a>\n        Myrtle Beach Marathon presented by\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chick-Fil-A" title="Chick-Fil-A">\n         Chick-Fil-A\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , every February featuring (since 2004) the Friday night\n       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Bank_of_Canada" title="Royal Bank of Canada">\n        Royal Bank of Canada\n       </a>\n       5K and the Saturday Dasani Half Marathon and Bi-Lo Marathon (from 1998 until 2008, a relay was held but dropped because of the popularity of the other events). Marathon day draws the limit of 6,000 runners annually (2,500 full, 3,500 half) and results usually in an unusual dawn as the race starts before dawn (6:30 AM) in order to finish by 2:30 PM.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/TicketReturn.com_Field" title="TicketReturn.com Field">\n        TicketReturn.com Field\n       </a>\n       at Pelicans Ballpark is the home field of the Myrtle Beach Pelicans and is located just off Highway 17 in Myrtle Beach. It opened in 1999 and seats 6,500 people. It is the finish point of the Bi-Lo Myrtle Beach Marathon. TicketReturn.com Field is also home of the annual "Baseball At The Beach" collegiate baseball tournament. Hosted by Coastal Carolina University each year, the tournament pits participating NCAA Division I baseball programs in the United States.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/NASCAR" title="NASCAR">\n        NASCAR\n       </a>\n       -sanctioned\n       <a href="/wiki/Stock_car_racing" title="Stock car racing">\n        Stock car racing\n       </a>\n       is held at\n       <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Beach_Speedway" title="Myrtle Beach Speedway">\n        Myrtle Beach Speedway\n       </a>\n       , a .538-mile (866\xc2\xa0m), semi-banked, asphalt-paved oval track located on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_501" title="US 501">\n        US 501\n       </a>\n       . Drivers in the Late Model classes will compete (against those of\n       <a href="/wiki/Greenville-Pickens_Speedway" title="Greenville-Pickens Speedway">\n        Greenville-Pickens Speedway\n       </a>\n       ) for the South Carolina Championship in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NASCAR_Whelen_All-American_Series" title="NASCAR Whelen All-American Series">\n        NASCAR Whelen All-American Series\n       </a>\n       . South Carolina Champions\' scores will be calculated against other state and provincial champions for a continental championship.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       It hosted the 2010 UOA Nationals where 8 collegiate ultimate teams from 5 conferences will be represented.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Golf">\n        Golf\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Golf">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The area is home to numerous golf courses and mini-golf courses along the Grand Strand and further inland. Myrtle Beach has been called the "Golf Capital of the World"\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       because of the roughly 100 golf courses located there, the record 4.2 million rounds played, and many miniature golf courses. 3.7 million total rounds of golf were played in 2007.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-myrtlebeachareachamber.com_22-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-myrtlebeachareachamber.com-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The majority of the area\'s golf courses are public. The Grand Strand is home of "\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hootie_and_the_Blowfish" title="Hootie and the Blowfish">\n        Hootie and the Blowfish\n       </a>\n       Day After the Masters Tournament". Extensive Chinese investment to the Myrtle Beach area golf market has resulted in a significant surge of Chinese tourists to the area and also resulted in 25+ golf courses being owned and/or operated by Chinese nationals.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Some of the notable golf courses and/or resorts include:\n      </p>\n      <table class="multicol" role="presentation"   </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government">\n        Government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The city of Myrtle Beach has a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Council-manager_government" title="Council-manager government">\n        council-manager government\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Mayor sits as a Council member-at-large and presides over\n       <a href="/wiki/City_council" title="City council">\n        City Council\n       </a>\n       meetings. In the event that the Mayor cannot preside over a City Council meeting, the Mayor Pro-Tem is the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chairman" title="Chairman">\n        presiding officer\n       </a>\n       of the meeting until such time as the Mayor returns to his seat. The City Manager is responsible for the administration and the day-to-day operation of all of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Municipal_services" title="Municipal services">\n        municipal services\n       </a>\n       and city departments. The City Manager also maintains intergovernmental relationships with federal, state, county and other\n       <a href="/wiki/Local_government" title="Local government">\n        local governments\n       </a>\n       . The city of Myrtle Beach reformed into a council-manager government system in 1974 under the administration of Mayor Bob Hirsch and city manager David Stradinger, who moved away from the city\'s former\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Strong_mayor" title="Strong mayor">\n        strong-mayor form\n       </a>\n       of government.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mayors">\n        Mayors\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Myrtle_Beach,_South_Carolina&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Mayors">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The current mayor of Myrtle Beach is John Rhodes, who has served since 2006.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr style="background:#ccc;">\n        <th>\n         <b>\n          Name\n         </b>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         <b>\n          From\n         </b>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         <b>\n          To\n         </b>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Dr. W.
